self = <queue3.DoublyLinkedList object at 0x7f04ea10dc30>
value = '[<queue3.DoublyLinkedList object at 0x7f04ea10dc30>]'

    def addAtHead(self, value: T) -> None:
    
        """Add node at head end."""
    
        if self.__size == 0:
            newNode = Node(value)
            self.__sentinel.next = newNode
            newNode.prev = self.__sentinel
            self.__tail = newNode
            self.__size += 1
        else:
            newNode = Node(value)
            nextNode = self.__sentinel.next
            self.__sentinel.next = newNode

    def addAtHead(self, value: T) -> None:
